<rate>4< /rate><gmapID>0x80d6fbd264e245cf:0xd62e1dd726890c61< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<resp>None</resp>< Review>
We have crossed the border at Andrade Port on foot and by vehicle, but almost always on foot. The port officers have always been very fair with our different situations, as much as can be expected. One time, we forgot to bring our passports, but they were practical, using our other picture I.D.s to support our American status. My wife is Filipino, but this didn't seem to change the fairness that we were given. The officers are firm and authoritative, as would be expected, but they are also kind and fair. I would never hesitate crossing, here and feel very safe. We have crossed close to 50 times over the past 15 years or so. We have dental work accomplished, as well as optometrist work. The city of Los Algodones is very safe and a great service to all who cross at Andrade Border crossing.<//Review>

I give these folks at this port of entry five stars.  Normally I would not be so complimentary but these people deserve it.  I recently crossed here - May 21st, 2019, to be exact - and I was stressed out as I did not really want to return to the soulless, sterile life of utterly meaningless competition and consumerism that is America today.  I stalled by the turnstille trying to verbally talk myself into crossing back into the US and finally just did it, trying to explain to the officer I encountered at their pedestrian lane counter that it's often hard for me to return to  the US and that such has nothing to do with my take on US CBP.  Miraculously, I was treated respectfully and the US  CBP officer allowed that she understood.  I was just amazed, absolutely amazed.  Beyond that, it was nice that my bags were not searched as they often have been at this port of entry in the past, though I had nothing on me I should not have, it was nice to be treated so respectfully and for once not as a criminal defendant as I was processed to re-enter the United States.  Way to go, Andrade Port of Entry  and keep up both the good and the respectful work!</Text>

< Review>
My girlfriend and I went here on the opening night. I've been to other Famous Dave's locations in Washington state, but this was the first time she had dined there.

We each ordered the 2 meat and 2 sides entree, and shared everything.  The highlights were the rib tips, cod, mac and cheese, beans, and garlic mashed potatoes.

We both enjoyed the meal and had leftovers to take home.  It took a while to be seated, but that's to be expected at a place that just opened.< /Review>

Not the best Chili's I've been to. Staff is generally very pleasant, but I find that they're only attentive to your table up until your main course arrives. At that point they are no where to be found except for their initial "How is everything?" at the two minute mark, most likely with food in your mouth, and barely giving you time to swallow and respond before wondering off to another table. The last meal I got there, took much longer than tables that were seated way after myself, the food came out lukewarm to cold, and then we were stuck there for days waiting to pay our tab and leave. Never will I step foot inside another Chilis establishment due to my experience at the Chilis in Modesto, CA.

I recently moved to the Modesto area from Florida and decided to grab some food and drinks with my sister.

We ordered drinks and as expected the server asked for our IDs, we handed her our Florida issued drivers licenses (we have not been here long enough to obtain CA IDs).¬†What I did not expect was for her to walk away with them with no explanation.¬†After about 5-10 mins, a different person approached us¬†with¬†our IDs and introduced herself as Heather, the manager, and stated that they were unable to accept our IDs and proceeded to explain her reasons:
1.	One of the IDs was cracked. She bends the ID as she attempts to show the "crack" that wasn't there.
2.	One of our IDs had a star and the other did not. SN: Florida licenses have changed within the past few years and each of ours were issued at different times. One is more current than the other. But both are VALID state issued IDs. The issue date is clearly printed on the front of the ID.
3.	It did not match the Florida ID in their "book". As explained in the 2nd reason, the state of Florida has more than one ID type therefore if we're going to be matching IDs to a "book" you need to have all IDs for each state.
At no point during this interaction did the manager offer to accommodate us for the inconvenience and her apology was artificial and insincere. Not willing to tolerate any further disrespect and unwarranted embarrassment we immediately left.

Since the time of the interaction I have spoken with Heather again via phone as well as Ken, the general manager, to understand their procedures and how they could allow potential customers to walk away upset, when we had done nothing wrong.

The attempt to give them an opportunity to at least¬†genuinely and sincerely apologize and or offer a reasonable explanation¬†lead nowhere with no attempt at a resolution on their part. I am infuriated at how poorly this situation was handled and will advise anyone I know against going to any Chilis establishment. Chilis Executives - please better train your management and staff on how to properly and respectfully handle interactions with customers.<//review>

<text>Okay Chili's.. Look. I love eating here, I love the Tropical Sunrise Margaritas and Priscilla (sp?) was a great server last night. We were not in her section, but she took us on anyways. It was about 9:00 last night 11/11/14. We went because, for one, we have been loyal customers for like ever now and absolutely love our experience every time. Two, it was Veterans Day so it was a win win for us. Great food, my fiance got his meal for free. Thank you! So. Anyways.. Let's get to the point. Give Priscilla a raise or something, she was awesome. Also that one guy that I think is a manager in that striped shirt, he was cool too. HOWEVER, like I have already said, I have been a loyal customer for a long time. I order the same thing, without fail, every single time I go in. I order a Tropical Sunrise Margarita, Triple Dipper and a Mushroom Swiss Burger. I can count on getting the same thing every time. I've had Chili's all the way from Modesto, Ca to Denver, Co. You guys are reliable, fast, friendly, courteous, etc. Well, after hundreds or dollars spent, I go in last night to spend another $50 bucks and order the Mushroom Swiss Burger. Oh but wait, THERE ARE NO MORE MUSHROOMS. WHAT!? Can you imagine my surprise? I had my order ready to go even before we got seated. Even before I even got off of work. I had to sit there and stare at the menu for what felt like forever just to figure out a way to cope with the loss of mushrooms. I am not someone to mix things up, but last night I was really thrown for a loop. There are literally no decent Mushroom Swiss Burgers anywhere in my area. Oh my Jesus. How do you just not have ANY mushrooms? For a brief moment, I was lost and confused. I felt like the whole world had come to a stop awaiting my decision. The fate of the world rest upon my shoulders and I had been so unprepared to do something else. I had no plan B. There was never a thought in my mind that I would have to do something different, to take a different route and change my path forever. No mushrooms, you say? Fine, I will bring my own next time.
